<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#160;7.01.</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top"> <p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Regulation FD Disclosure.</p></td></tr></table> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On December&#160;14, 2021, 3M Company (&#8220;3M&#8221;) and Neogen Corporation (&#8220;Neogen&#8221;) issued a joint press release announcing the execution of certain definitive agreements providing for a combination of Neogen and the Food Safety Department of 3M on the terms and conditions set forth in such agreements. A copy of the joint press release is furnished as Exhibit 99 hereto and incorporated herein by reference.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Important Information About the Transaction and Where to Find It</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with the proposed transaction, Neogen and Garden SpinCo Corporation, a wholly owned subsidiary of 3M (&#8220;Garden SpinCo&#8221;), intend to file registration statements with the SEC. Neogen will also file a proxy statement. 3M stockholders are urged to read the prospectus and/or information statement that will be included in the registration statements and any other relevant documents when they become available, and Neogen stockholders are urged to read the proxy statement and any other relevant documents when they become available, because they will contain important information about Neogen, Garden SpinCo, 3M and the proposed transactions. The proxy statement, prospectus and/or information statement and other documents relating to the proposed transactions (when they become available) can also be obtained free of charge from the SEC&#8217;s website at www.sec.gov. The proxy statement, prospectus and/or information statement and other documents (when they are available) can also be obtained free of charge from 3M upon written request to 3M Investor Relations Department, Bldg. <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">224-1W-02,</span></span> St. Paul, MN 55144, or by <span style="white-space:nowrap">e-mailing</span> investorrelations@3M.com or upon written request to Neogen&#8217;s Investor Relations, 620 Lesher Place, Lansing, Michigan 48912 or by <span style="white-space:nowrap">e-mailing</span> ir@neogen.com.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Participants in the Solicitation</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This communication is not a solicitation of a proxy from any security holder of Neogen. However, Neogen, 3M and certain of their respective directors and executive officers may be deemed to be participants in the solicitation of proxies from shareholders of Neogen in connection with the proposed transaction under the rules of the SEC. Information regarding the persons who are, under the rules of the SEC, participants in the solicitation of the stockholders of Neogen in connection with the proposed transactions, including a description of their direct or indirect interests, by security holdings or otherwise, will be set forth in the proxy statement/prospectus when it is filed with the SEC. Information about the directors and executive officers of 3M may be found in its Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> filed with the SEC on February&#160;4, 2021, and its definitive proxy statement relating to its 2021 Annual Meeting of Shareholders filed with the SEC on March&#160;24, 2021. Information about the directors and executive officers of Neogen may be found in its Annual Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">10-K</span> filed with the SEC on July&#160;30, 2021, and its definitive proxy statement relating to its 2021 Annual Meeting of Stockholders filed with the SEC on August&#160;31, 2021.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">No Offer or Solicitation</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This communication is not intended to and shall not constitute an offer to sell or the solicitation of an offer to sell or the solicitation of an offer to buy any securities or a solicitation of any vote of approval, nor shall there be any sale of securities in any jurisdiction in which such offer, solicitation or sale would be unlawful prior to registration or qualification under the securities laws of any such jurisdiction. No offer of securities shall be made except by means of a prospectus meeting the requirements of Section&#160;10 of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#160;9.01 &#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;Financial Statements and Exhibits.</p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) Exhibits.</p> <p style="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Announcement Press Release </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NEOGEN to Combine 3M&#146;s Food Safety Business With its Existing Operations, Creating a Global Industry Leader </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Creates a pure play Food Security company with pro forma revenue of approximately $1&nbsp;billion and Adjusted EBITDA of approximately
$300&nbsp;million expected in its first full year post-closing. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Pro forma company expected to have stronger growth through
substantial cross synergies in product innovation, sales, marketing, distribution and production; an EBITDA margin profile of approximately 30% and increased exposure to higher growth, lower volatility Food Safety
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">end-markets</FONT> which will represent approximately 70% of total revenue. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Combined company will
have the enhanced geographic footprint, innovative product offerings, digitization capabilities, and financial flexibility to capitalize on robust growth trends in sustainability, food safety and supply chain integrity. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>Intended <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-efficient</FONT> transaction will result in 3M shareholders owning 50.1% of NEOGEN and
existing NEOGEN shareholders owning 49.9%. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><I>3M to receive consideration valued at approximately $1&nbsp;billion, subject to closing
and other adjustments. </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">LANSING, Mich., and ST. PAUL, Minn., December&nbsp;14, 2021 &#150; NEOGEN Corporation (NASDAQ: NEOG) and 3M (NYSE: MMM)
announced today that they have entered into a definitive agreement pursuant to which 3M will separate its Food Safety business and simultaneously combine it with NEOGEN in a transaction that is intended to be
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-efficient</FONT> to 3M and its shareholders for U.S. federal income tax purposes. The combination will create an innovative leader in the food safety sector with a comprehensive product range and a strategic
focus on the category&#146;s long-term growth opportunities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The transaction implies an enterprise value for 3M&#146;s Food Safety business of
approximately $5.3&nbsp;billion, including $1&nbsp;billion in new debt to be incurred by 3M&#146;s Food Safety business. This represents an implied multiple of approximately 32x and 27x CY 2022E Adjusted EBITDA pre and post <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">run-rate</FONT> synergies respectively, based on NEOGEN&#146;s closing price as of December&nbsp;13, 2021. 3M&#146;s Food Safety business will fund to 3M consideration valued at approximately $1&nbsp;billion, subject to
closing and other adjustments. The combined company is expected to have an enterprise value of approximately $9.3&nbsp;billion, based on NEOGEN&#146;s closing share price as of December&nbsp;13, 2021. Under the terms of the definitive agreements,
which involve a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-free</FONT> &#147;Reverse Morris Trust&#148; structure, existing NEOGEN shareholders will continue to own approximately 49.9% of the combined company, and 3M shareholders will receive
approximately 50.1% of the combined company. The Boards of Directors of both NEOGEN and 3M have unanimously approved the transaction. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;This
combination will enhance NEOGEN&#146;s position in this new era of food security, equipping us with an expanded product line that enables us to capitalize on our growing footprint, reaching more customers, more often, while continuing our track
record of strong and consistent growth,&#148; said John Adent, NEOGEN&#146;s President and Chief Executive Officer. &#147;The heightened global focus on food security, sustainability and supply chain solutions around the world presents exciting
opportunities for NEOGEN to be positioned as an innovative leader at the forefront of the growth and digitization of the industry. We&#146;re excited to welcome 3M&#146;s Food Safety employees to the NEOGEN team, and we&#146;re looking forward to
demonstrating the immense benefits of this combination to our customers, employees and shareholders.&#148; </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;NEOGEN and 3M share a deep commitment to quality, innovation and customer satisfaction and long
histories of industry leadership. By combining our Food Safety business with NEOGEN, we will create an organization well positioned to capture long-term profitable growth. This transaction further evolves our strategy, focuses our health care
business and benefits our stakeholders, as we actively manage our portfolio to drive growth and deliver shareholder value<I>,&#148; </I>said Mike Roman, 3M Chairman and Chief Executive Officer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>An Innovative Global Leader in Food Safety: Key Strategic Benefits </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The combination is expected to generate significant long-term value for shareholders of the combined company, as well as customers and employees by: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Creating a leading innovator in an industry benefiting from growing demand:</B> NEOGEN&#146;s pure play food
security business, combined with the long-term tailwinds of increased global focus on sustainability, food safety and supply chain solutions, mean NEOGEN is the ideal home for 3M&#146;s Food Safety business. A combination will create a global
innovator in food safety with the geographic footprint, product range and innovation capabilities to further capitalize on attractive and enduring growth trends. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Expanding food safety product offerings to better serve customers: </B>The company will have a significantly
expanded product offering in food safety, particularly in indicator testing and pathogen detection areas, which complement NEOGEN&#146;s existing microbiology lines. NEOGEN will also be able to offer 3M food safety customers its genomics services,
which deliver innovative DNA testing &#150; a new offering to 3M food safety customers. This expanded product range, along with NEOGEN&#146;s complementary animal safety business, increases the solutions with which NEOGEN helps customers protect the
world&#146;s food supply from the farm gate to the dinner plate. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Generating global growth opportunities: </B>The combined company creates an opportunity to optimize NEOGEN
and 3M Food Safety&#146;s high-growth capabilities to add value for customers through a compelling product offering. Beyond the U.S. and Europe,<B> </B>heightened interest in developing nations in improving food safety presents significant growth
potential for the combined company. The combination will also provide investment flexibility to pursue international expansion. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Creating a compelling offering through enhanced R&amp;D capabilities, innovation and analytics:</B> NEOGEN
is looking to the future of the industry, and with 3M&#146;s Food Safety business, will possess the breadth and digital capabilities to lead the digitization of the food security industry. The complementary product offerings combined with
NEOGEN&#146;s data-driven analytics approach will create a compelling solution as customers seek innovative partners to increase efficiency and enhance food safety protocols. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Enhancing revenue, margin and earnings stability:</B> The combined company is expected to have an improved
financial profile, which is expected to further enhance NEOGEN&#146;s already consistently high-performing revenue stream with improved EBITDA margins by increasing exposure to highly profitable food safety categories and providing substantial <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">run-rate</FONT> growth and cost synergies of approximately $30&nbsp;million in EBITDA contribution. These </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="9%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
synergies are expected to be achieved by the end of year three following the close of transaction through efficiencies in product innovation, sales, marketing, distribution and production. The
combination will boost NEOGEN&#146;s food safety segment to approximately 70% of total revenue post-transaction, with total projected pro forma revenues of approximately $1&nbsp;billion expected in the first full year post closing. Pro forma EBITDA
is expected to be approximately $300&nbsp;million with a higher overall EBITDA margin profile of approximately 30% expected in the first full year post closing. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Transaction Details </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The transaction involves a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-free</FONT> &#147;Reverse Morris Trust&#148; transaction structure, where 3M&#146;s Food Safety business will be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">spun-off</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">split-off</FONT> to
3M shareholders and simultaneously merged with a wholly owned subsidiary of NEOGEN. The transaction is intended to be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">tax-efficient</FONT> to 3M and 3M&#146;s shareholders for U.S. federal income tax purposes. At the
completion of the transaction, NEOGEN will issue a number of shares to 3M shareholders such that 3M shareholders will receive approximately 50.1% of the combined company and existing NEOGEN shareholders will continue to own approximately 49.9% of
the combined company. In connection with the transaction, 3M will also receive consideration valued at approximately $1&nbsp;billion, subject to closing and other adjustments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NEOGEN&#146;s expected pro forma net leverage ratio at close is expected to be less than 2.5x, inclusive of the $1&nbsp;billion of new debt. Strong expected
free cash flow generation and EBITDA growth of the combined business enables rapid deleveraging post-closing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The transaction is expected to close by the
end of Q3 2022, subject to approval by NEOGEN shareholders, receipt of required regulatory approvals and the satisfaction of other customary closing conditions. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Leadership and Governance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NEOGEN&#146;s President and
Chief Executive Officer, John Adent, and NEOGEN&#146;s existing management team will continue to lead the combined company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The size of the NEOGEN board
will be increased and two new independent board members, to be designated by 3M, will be appointed at closing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call and Investor
Information </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NEOGEN and 3M will together hold a webcast today, December&nbsp;14, at 8:00 AM ET to discuss this announcement. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Advisors </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Centerview Partners LLC is serving as exclusive financial advisor and Weil, Gotshal&nbsp;&amp; Manges LLP is serving as legal counsel to NEOGEN. </P>

Goldman Sachs Bank USA and JP Morgan Securities are providing committed financing for the transaction. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">### </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About NEOGEN </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NEOGEN Corporation develops and markets
comprehensive solutions dedicated to food and animal safety. The company&#146;s Food Safety segment markets dehydrated culture media and diagnostic test kits to detect foodborne bacteria, natural toxins, food allergens, drug residues, plant
diseases, and sanitation concerns. NEOGEN&#146;s Animal Safety segment is a leader in the development of genomic solutions along with the manufacturing and distribution of a variety of animal healthcare products, including diagnostics,
pharmaceuticals, veterinary instruments, wound care, and disinfectants, as well as rodent and insect control solutions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About 3M </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At 3M (NYSE: MMM), we apply science in collaborative ways to improve lives daily as our employees connect with customers all around the world. Learn more about
3M&#146;s creative solutions to global challenges at www.3M.com or on Twitter @3M or @3MNews. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Cautionary Notes on Forward Looking Statements </B></P>
